COURSE: Duality
AUTHOR: Jeffrey Allen
====================

Preparation

==============================

Preparation – Welcome to Duality Quest

<v ->When I had my first experiences with energy awareness and
intuition, I wasn’t even sure these things were real, or if I believed
in energy at all. At the time, I was finishing degrees in Computer
Science and Mathematics, and I’d already landed a job with the U.S.
Department of Energy, which is a whole different kind of energy. And I
was sure the path to success was hard work and a sharp mind. I wasn’t
really looking for anything else, but out of the blue, I started having
unusual experiences that I couldn’t explain. I was seeing light around
people, and speaking telepathically, and having these spontaneous energy
healing experiences. And honestly, I didn’t know what to think, but the
scientist in me couldn’t just ignore my experiences. So I did what any
good scientist would do. I started learning and experimenting more, but
mostly I kept these experiences to myself, so people wouldn’t think I
was a little crazy, or kind of going off the deep end. And over the next
15 years, my life really followed these two parallel paths. By day, I
was a software engineer, working up through the ranks, making money, and
succeeding at the American dream. And by night, I was studying
everything I could find about intuition and energy healing. I completed
clairvoyant training, and graduate studies, and energy work, and healing
apprenticeships, and trance mediumship training, and clairvoyant
teachers training, and so on. And I even served on the Board of
Directors for Psychic Horizons Center, which was the local clairvoyant
training school that I went to. And I lived in these two very different
worlds, but I didn’t really see it that way. For me, all of life was my
energy playground. I worked on energy in meetings at work, and in my
relationships, and for my health. And even when I was driving my car, or
eating, or exercising, I was totally fascinated by what we can do with
energy. And the fact that no one seemed to know about it, that part
really surprised me. And eventually I was teaching a little on the
weekends, and doing some healings after work, but this was all really
just a hobby until I started to see how much I was helping people. And
suddenly my computer job, even with all its money and success, seemed
kind of silly and even a little selfish. I was making more impact in the
world in a few hours with my hobby than an entire month in my real job.
And suddenly I saw this bigger potential for my life, and energetically,
I leaned into it. And by 2005, my life had completely changed. Energy
work was my career, and engineering was my hobby. And I used all the
energy tools that I’d learned to discover a whole new life for myself. I
became a full-time energy healer, intuitive, and teacher. And I used my
engineering mind to organize everything I learned into a system for
teaching intuition, and healing to others. It was great. And for the
next 10 years, teaching became my classroom where I learned what worked,
and what didn’t work to help others heal themselves, and access their
intuition. I tied energy healing and intuition around the world, and
founded my own teaching center in Japan. But again, I started to feel
like I was playing kind of small. I knew I could help so many more
people with the programs that I was developing. Again, I saw this bigger
potential for my life, and I leaned into it energetically. That’s when I
met Vishen and Mindvalley at A-Fest in Thailand. And Vishen was talking
about his vision for changing education, and upleveling human
consciousness. And I knew I wanted to help. Before long, I was working
on the Duality training with Mindvalley, using all the energy tools and
teaching techniques that I’d learned over the years, and adding one more
important piece that was missing. The why. Why would people want to
learn intuition and energy healing? How could each tool help them in
their daily life? What problems could they solve? How could they improve
their lives? How would this impact their relationships, and their
families in the world? It may sound silly, but until Vishen asked me
these things, I never thought about them. I was usually preaching to the
choir to people who were already interested in energy work, but Vishen
wanted to reach everyone, including people who didn’t know anything
about energy yet. And I thought, wow, now that’s bigger potential. And
this focus on energy and tangible practical benefits in everyday life is
what makes Duality different from other energy training, and spiritual
training that I’ve seen. Duality really is graduate level energy
training that anyone can digest. And it ties directly into your daily
life. People are drawn to energy work and spirituality for many reasons.
For some, it’s personal. Maybe you’re at a crossroads, and you’re tired
of life as usual, or you feel kind of stuck or hopeless, or just plain
bored with your life. You want to try something different, break out of
your box, and create a new life for yourself. But you don’t want to join
a cult, or change your religion. If this is you, Duality will help. You
can explore energy healing firsthand, and see tangible results for
yourself. And then you can decide what’s real for you. For many people,
energy healing is about relating to others. You want to communicate
better, improve your relationships, or have better boundaries, so you
can feel more comfortable around other people. Or maybe you’re tired of
getting in arguments, and you want to polish some of your rough edges,
so you can really enjoy your time with others. When you understand the
energy of how we relate to each other, all these things are possible,
because relationships are all about energy exchange. Or maybe a higher
calling is drawing you to energy healing. You may want to help people,
and make a big difference in the world, or if you’re already helping
people, you may want to refine your talents, and learn new tools to
engage even more powerfully. And we’ll do that in Duality. In fact,
these three motivations, self, others, and the world are how the Duality
training is organized, because it’s how our energy awareness naturally
progresses. In chapters one, two, and three, you’ll explore how energy
affects you personally. You’ll learn energy tools for grounding and
personal presence, mental clarity and focus, and healing, and energizing
your body. These are the tools which accelerate your growth, and help
you get through life’s difficult transitions. As you see results from
healing yourself, the next natural step is to work on how you relate
with others energetically. And that’s chapters four and five. You’ll
learn how to adjust your aura, create healthy boundaries energetically,
so that you’re not an energy sponge, and you’re not like a prickly pear.
You’re just comfortable and approachable energetically. You’ll learn how
the chakras talk with people, which is even stronger than body language.
And how chakra healing can help you manifest your dreams. And then once
you’re feeling good about you, and you’re feeling good about your
relationships, it’s time to peek behind the curtain, and see how you fit
into the world. In chapter six, you learn where your beliefs are stored
energetically, and how to see the world through a completely different
lens. And this is critical, because you’re getting ready to live your
life in a whole new way. You must open your mind to do this. In chapter
seven, you learn to refine your intuition. So you can lead a life of
synchronicity and abundance, where you’re creating and flowing, instead
of feeling stuck or struggling. And finally, in chapter eight, we pull
the curtain back all the way. And we look at who you truly are as a
spirit, as you learn to access your higher self, and your higher
guidance. Now this may sound like a tall order right now, but I will
guide you every step of the way. And by the time you’ve been through the
first seven chapters, it’ll be a lot easier than you think. You can do
this. I’ve taught intuition and energy healing to thousands of people
all around the world. And from what I’ve seen, everyone is intuitive.
Everyone is a healer. Everyone is amazing. And that includes you. To
access your natural healing abilities, all you need is a willingness to
try it out, a little time each day to learn step by step, the sense of
humor for when things don’t go as you expect, and a commitment to see it
through, a commitment to find out what you can really do. And there will
be times when resistance comes up in you. That’s normal, because you’re
growing, but just keep going. I can’t tell you how many times students
have told me, I was just about to drop out, and the very next lesson
said exactly what I needed to hear. You got this. You can tap into the
intuition and energy healing abilities, which are already within you.
You just need to lean in to your potential, and I’ll show you how.

LESSON 2: Your Body & Spirit Connection for Personal Presence

<v ->Welcome back, give yourself a deep breath, and say hello to the
group energy. Send smiles and hellos to your fellow students and feel
the group energy and intention supporting you. Very good, today I want
to answer an important question, what’s the number one reason why people
can’t sense energy? I’ve heard a lot of good guesses, but the truth
might surprise you. The number one reason people can’t sense energy is
that they’re not present in their body, it’s that simple. Now this might
seem funny because we’re talking about energy awareness, but if you’re
not present in your body, it’s very hard to sense energy, and I know
this from experience. I had my first experiences with energy in 1990. I
was my last year of college, I was getting a BS in Mathematics and a BS
in Computer Science. And I had a few profound energy experiences and I
didn’t really know what to make of them, but they were really exciting.
So I started to study about energy and I was reading books, and
listening to channelers and by the mid ’90s, I was full on new age. I
was rejecting the physical world and attempting to be more spiritual. So
I had lots of restrictions on what I could eat and what I could drive or
drink, and so on and I had a lot of spiritual ideas, but honestly, I
didn’t have many energy experiences. And I do remember one exception
though, it was in 1995 and it was this stormy night and everything’s
rattling in the house and I heard this, this voice and I finally said,
okay, what, what are you trying to tell me? What are you trying to say?
And I got this really clear message said, “Go to Malkuth, there you will
find unprecedented clarity of thought and peace of mind, use it to save
the world.” And I woke up and kind of wrote it on the notepad next to
the phone, and in the morning, I was like, wow, this is real, I can’t
believe it, I got this message. And Malkuth must be this magical place
where I’m going to go get some magical awareness, all right. And I
started searching around and I was looking in libraries and on maps and
this is before the internet was around, so it was a little harder, I
couldn’t find it, even though I was really searching and I got really
disappointed. But years later, I discovered that Malkuth is actually the
bottom node on the Kabbalistic tree of life and it represents the body.
My guidance was just saying, get in your body, but I didn’t understand.
Now a few years later, in 1997, I found Psychic Horizon Center which is
this fantastic energy training school and I tried to sign up for their
astral travel class. Again, I was thinking if I got out of my body, I
was going to find some amazing information. Now, fortunately, they told
me you can’t take that, it’s a graduate class, and we recommend this
intuition and energy healing very much like what I’m teaching you right
now. And they knew that this idea of getting out of the body was not
going to work for me, so they steered me towards something that would
help me get into my body. About a year later, I remember I had my first
real experience of being in my body and I was shocked, it felt really
heavy and slow and really aware and relaxed and powerful, kind of like a
Neo in “The Matrix”. You know that scene where suddenly he’s like,
everything slows down and he’s blocking bullets, so it kind of felt like
that, my world was suddenly in 3D and it never had been before. And
since that time, I’ve had so many more energy experiences because I’m
present in my body, and this is a common confusion that many people
have. We believe in a world of opposites and we think that the body is
the opposite of the spirit, but yes, we have a body and yes, we have a
spirit, but no, they’re not in competition. Becoming more spiritual
isn’t about becoming less physical or restricting the physical or taking
anything away, in fact, less body focus just makes us more spaced out,
we have less energy awareness. And again, I know because I got really
spaced out and I got really woo-woo, I’ve been there. So your goal in
this training is really mastering both, it’s not a competition between
your body and your spirit. So you don’t have to be less physical or eat
less meat or have less possessions or less money to be more spiritual.
Spirituality doesn’t replace your physical awareness, it just augments
it. So you can change your experience and perception even if you don’t
change your situation, even ascension is not about getting out of your
body. This might sound kind of funny, but ascension is actually about
getting better integrated within your body. So your body is ascending or
becoming more coherent, but your spirit is descending or fitting into
the body, but of course, we can’t sell dissension workshops ’cause you
know, it’s not sexy, so we talk about ascension. So what does it look
like to really be in the body? So think about people who you really
admire. They probably have a strong personal presence and they probably
inspire you to be present too, like powerful speakers, like Martin
Luther king or Lisa Nichols. You might think of athletes in the zone, so
when somebody’s passing a ball, they’re totally focused in the body, in
that moment. You might think of a singer or a dancer or a performer,
they have to be so present in the body or actors, they’re so present in
the body that we can cry and celebrate about their fake situations that
aren’t even real. You can also think about strong public figures like
Obama, very present in the body or newborn babies, newborn babies are
very present. So when you think about this, what do all these people
have in common? They probably have a passion for what they’re doing,
they have a strong focus, they have confidence or expertise and they’re
present in their body. So such people also report having strong
intuition and guidance. So let’s think of some examples in your life
too. Maybe you’re having a deep conversation and you’re really
interested, or maybe you’re playing sports, you feel really motivated or
you’re doing yoga and you feel so focused, or maybe you’re performing
something, you’re sharing your expertise, maybe you’re just having a
moment of physical intimacy and you’re very present, or you’re out in
nature in this high coherence space and you’re becoming more present. My
point is that you already know how to be powerfully present, so why
aren’t you doing it all the time? I really want you to get this, that
personal presence simply means your spirit is more present in your body.
In all these situations, people are present in their body with their
attention, their awareness and their energy. And you’ve heard a lot of
sayings like this, be in the moment, live in the present, be here now.
So to me, these are all saying, be present in your body. From an energy
perspective, your physical body is your here and now, it’s the only part
of you which has a position here at a timeframe, now. So then what are
you? It’s common for people to think I am my body or I am my thoughts,
or I am my mind and it’s even getting popular to think I am
consciousness and my body is a vehicle, but this is a little funny too

in that space where they were just shopping, didn’t want to buy, kind of

backcountry snowboard, both of which come with some risks. And I
remember rock climbing one time in Estes Park, Colorado, and we’re on
this route. I’m having a good time. It was a friction slab, which means

from your hands and your feet. And I’m heading up the climb and I’m on
this little spot where I’m just holding on a little thing about the size
of a peanut with one hand, and my right foot’s just on this little tiny
slope, and my other hand and foot are just kind of flailing for balance.
There’s nothing to hold on to. And I thought to myself, “Okay, I could
use a little protection right now.” So I’m a free climber, which means I
put my own gear in as I go up. And before I went up, I could see where I
put the gear, but I was nowhere near it. This round was actually going
at an angle. On this kind of climb, you can’t really choose where you
go. There’s just, you have to go with the flow. And at that point I
realized, “Oh, this,”this doesn’t have any gear.” My mind flashed back
to the book, there’s a 9X climb in the book. An X means if you fall, you
know, X, it’s all over. And I never climb stuff like this, but I
happened to find myself in the middle of this one and I was starting to
come out of my body, my attention was going everywhere. I went down to
the last piece of pro that I put in, the last protection, and I realized
it’s behind a little flake, which is going to break at this distance and

piece popped. So I realized, “Oh, great.”So if I fall, I’m going to take

of your body when you’re sleeping too. You know, you’re actually going
off to a little bit different dimension. When you’re drunk, that gets
you out of your body and out of your pain, which is probably why people
like to do it. And, of course, you know, after life. So when you have no
more body, you’re not in it. So you’re probably starting to see a
pattern here. If being in the body feels good, then why aren’t we
present all the time? Sometimes it’s fear. It doesn’t feel good, so we
don’t want to be present for it. But in this case, your body probably
needs you to be present. It’s hard to make good decisions if you’re not
in your body. Pain is another big reason we’re not in our body. It also
doesn’t feel good and we don’t want to be present. You might have some
distractions like the TV or the phone or YouTube, or maybe a lack of
passion and interest in your life. These feelings tend to make us want
to float away. Self-judgment is a big one. If you think, “My nose is too
big, or my butt is too small,”or I’m too tall or too short,” or
whatever, you don’t have a good relationship between your spirit and
your body. And I recommend letting these ideas go because when you have
a good relationship with your body, it’s easier to be grounded and in
the body. All right? Whew! So we’re starting to get a little ungrounded
as I give all those examples, so let’s go ahead and change that. So just
think to yourself right now, what does strong presence look like to you?
Think of some people that you really admire. They probably have a strong
personal presence and they inspire you to be present too. I like to
think about this guy, Konishiki Yasokichi. He was the world’s heaviest
Sumo Wrestler. He’s from Hawaii. Now, this guy was 285 kilogram. That’s
over 630 pounds. So look at this face. He’s like 150% present. I don’t
want to face that guy. And I should probably mention here that while
gaining weight does help you ground, grounding energetically doesn’t
make you gain weight. So don’t worry about that. Remember our other
great examples too. Athletes in the zone, powerful speakers, singers,
dancers, performers, actors that can make you cry and jump for joy, even
though their stories aren’t real, spiritual leaders like a Yogi or the
Dalai Lama. These are our role models for personal presence and
oftentimes, they’re role models for great decision-making and positive
change too. Think about it. In his lifetime, Nelson Mandela helped South
Africa break out of a very strong negative feedback loop and begin
moving into a positive feedback loop instead. Everything is possible.
Next, I’d like to share a different way of learning about being in the
body. So we’ll take a little journey into the earth and then back to
your body. I always imagine an elevator for this journey, but if
elevators make you uncomfortable, feel free to imagine a beautiful ball
of light instead. That’ll work too. So let’s begin. Go ahead and close
your eyes. Give yourself a deep breath. Be grounded, present, and
relaxed in your body. Call back all your energy from other times and
places, and be fully present behind your eyes. Breathe. And notice the
earth beneath you. Feel your energy extending from the base of your
spine, deep into the earth. And as you connect with the earth, feel your
body relax. Feel your grounding to the earth getting stronger and
becoming as wide as your body. Notice any tension in your body and give
it permission to release. Breathe. And let your grounding expand further
until it’s as wide as your outstretched arms. Now imagine that you’re in
a round glass elevator inside this large grounding. You’re going to ride
this elevator down to the center of the earth. So press that down button
now and feel the elevator, and feel that bubble of energy starting to
move. Feel your awareness moving down through your body, past your feet
and down into the earth. Continue moving down deeper and deeper into the
earth, and notice any thoughts which distract you from this journey and
just let them release. Breathe. Feel yourself arriving at a large cave
in the center of the earth. See a soft light radiating from the walls of
the cave, illuminating the space around you. Feel the pulsating energy
of the earth all around. Ask the earth to give you a deep healing right
now. Let yourself relax and receive this healing. Feel any old long-held
pains releasing from your body. Feel your anxiety and worries release.
Feel your doubts about yourself sinking into the earth, releasing from
you forever. And ask the earth if there’s anything else that can help
you heal. Be grateful to receive this healing from the earth. Breathe.
Feel the earth’s energy getting stronger beneath you. Feel it lifting
your elevator, pushing you up through the earth again. As you travel
upward, notice the earth energy filling and cleaning your grounding.
Feel yourself arriving again in your body. Moving past your heart and
your throat, and let your awareness be gently right behind your eyes.
See that elevator fade and disappear and feel your grounding become as
wide as your body again. Notice how your body feels being strongly
connected to the earth, and feel your spirit being fully present and
deeply anchored into your body. Give yourself a deep breath. Smile. Be
confident, relaxed, and clear. Wiggle your hands and feet. Stretch. Open
your eyes and come out of trance. So take a few moments by yourself to
get used to this strong grounding in your body. Enjoy.

Part 2: Gain Mental & Intuitive Clarity

LESSON 7: Cultivating Intuition & a Balanced Mind

<v ->Welcome, everyone. It’s Jeffrey Allen again. Before we begin,
please remember your grounding and say hello to the earth energy. Send
smiles and hellos to your fellow students. And feel the group energy and
intention supporting you. Very good. In this chapter, we’re talking
about mental and intuitive clarity, about cultivating a balanced mind.
Now, of course, we all want clarity, but sometimes it’s difficult to
find. So what can we do energetically to find clarity? Well, first we
need to realize that finding answers is different than finding objects.
To find something in the physical world we usually become active, and
put in effort, and we’re searching. So we might be looking around for a
lost wallet or looking for a new pair of shoes, and if we don’t do
anything we’re less likely to find the object. By contrast, to find
something in the energy world we just ask. And then we wait, and we
listen, and we trust the timing. If we don’t do anything we’re actually
more likely to find the answer. There’s a great parable from “Crying
About This,” where there’s a man walking down the road and he sees this
fork in the road up ahead. And he knows, “Ah, this is really important.
I need to know which way to go, but I don’t know what to do.” So he’s
walking toward it, he’s getting stressed out, and at some point, he
stops. And he’s just thinking, and thinking, and analyzing, you know,
“Which way should I go, which one’s the right way?” And eventually, he
keeps going, there’s no answers, and finally sits down and he meditates,
gets really calm. Meditates, tries to find that answer. Still nothing.
No answer. So at this point, he’s running out of time. He kind of gives
up and in despair, he’s walking up toward the fork in the road. And then
when he gets to the fork, there’s a little sign that just says, “Go this
way.” And this is how energy works. All that effort didn’t help because
he didn’t have the right timing. And our answers come when we need them
not before. So this frustrates a lot of people who want to get the
answers right away. You might be wondering, why are these things so
different? Why are finding objects and finding answers so different?
Well, we’re not physically connected to all objects, but we are
energetically connected to all energy. And we’ll try out that connection
today, but you might be thinking, aren’t objects energy too? Okay, yeah,
pretty clever. And as it turns out, these energy tools and energy tricks
do work in the physical world too. So, for example, if you lose your
wallet, you can look for it energetically. You just ground the wallet
and then look for the grounding cord instead. Or you might go shopping
and just ask for the shoes ahead of time. And then you’re out, you’ve
forgotten about it, and they kind of magically appear in the store
window. Have you ever had that happen? You can also ask your parking
angels to find a great parking spot for you or to change the stoplights
to green for you, and these things work. But most people don’t think to
try them out. Keep in mind, intuition and sensing energy requires deep
listening, and it requires trust and patience, but intuition and sensing
energy doesn’t require effort or stress. It doesn’t require a perfect
track record or perfect abilities. You can just start doing things
differently now and you’ll find a new awareness comes on pretty quickly.
Some people ask me, “When did you start using your intuition?” And it’s
funny because I remember thinking, “I can’t do it. I can’t do it. I
can’t do it.” And then one day I just noticed, “Oh, I’m doing it.” And
then I realized, “Oh, I think I was always doing it, I just wasn’t aware
that I was doing it.” And this brings me to this chapter’s big question,
which is, what’s the number one reason why we can’t hear our intuition?
So what do you think? Maybe talent, or training, or practice, or because
you don’t live in Sedona. Actually, the number one reason why we can’t
hear our intuition is too much noise. So I’ve trained many students who
said, “I can’t see,” or “I can’t hear,” and this is not a skills or
sensitivity problem. It’s almost always a too much noise problem. So if
you imagine you’re with a friend in an intimate quiet setting, and
you’re having a conversation, it’s easy to hear them, right? And now
imagine that same friend, you’re in a crowded elevator with other
people, and everybody’s talking, it’s kind of hard to hear that friend,
isn’t it? Is possible, but it’s hard. Now imagine a live concert and
it’s impossible to hear anything, but the music. Your internal noise is
very similar. It’s often blocking your calm, quiet, intuitive voice. So
what’s the biggest source of internal noise. It’s your brain and
overthinking. Like the live concert, it’s too much of a good thing. Now
I know from experience, I’m a chronic overthinker. My mind can be very
loud. I can give you many examples from my life. When my mind gets
whirling, I start to notice details and unimportant patterns like the
floor tiles, or the ceiling tiles, which one’s out of place, or how they
could be better. It’s kind of like a monk on a TV show, but, you know,
not as brilliant. And I might get stuck in extreme precision where
everything has to be precisely arranged or perfectly done. When we’re
overthinking, we want the right way or the perfect answer for
everything. Like where exactly is the root chakra? How many centimeters
wide is my grounding? I get these questions a lot. And such precision is
actually not important for energy work and for many other things too. If
you don’t know what I’m talking about, like hand chakras or so on, don’t
worry about it. Just kind of go with it. Don’t think. Another example of
overthinking is overplanning your words. So you’re not really listening
to anyone else in the conversation. You’re just kind of waiting for a
break in the conversation so you can start talking again. Or sometimes
we imagine a long series of negative cause and effect. Like one time my
wife, Hisami, had a shoulder injury that was healing. And I was really
worried about her moving it around. And so my mind got a little crazy
and I told her, “You know, if you move your arm, it’s not going to heal.
And if it doesn’t heal, you’re not going to be able to work and if you
can’t work, you’re not going to be able to make money. And if you can’t
make money, you’re going to be homeless.” And I guess, you know, I
thought this was going to motivate her somehow, but it just made me seem
kind of crazy. And, of course, she was just laughing at me. When our
minds are overactive, sometimes we tell stories like this. We tell
stories about people that we don’t know. Now, this is not me personally,
but I’ve had several clients that will tell me, “I saw the same man
three times, maybe he’s following me or maybe he’s secretly in love with
me.” And you can probably think of some fun examples in your life too,
right? Maybe some songs playing in your head, or you can’t stop thinking
about something, or you’re obsessing about some small detail. We all do
this sometimes. Overthinking may not seem like a big deal, but the
results can actually be very big. It can lead to difficulties in
personal or work relationships. Maybe it’ll be viewed as critical or
judgmental, even though it’s not intentional. Or maybe you tend to see
things as black and white, right and wrong, good and bad. You might find
yourself arguing about unimportant things. My friend and his girlfriend
used to have huge fights about whether the drawers in the kitchen were
100% closed or not. This is not an important detail. Overthinking also
makes it hard to make decisions and to finish projects, it can create
stress-related health concerns, and my adrenals were it shot by the time
I was in my mid-30s, you also might become a poor listener and tend to
think that you’re always right, or he might have trouble visualizing or
sensing energy. Sound familiar? It’s hard to sense energy if you’re
always thinking about things. Now, there’s nothing wrong with using your
brain, thinking is great, but you want to balance intuition with your
thinking. So tell your brain then, instead of balancing pros and cons,
and rights and wrongs, it can start balancing thinking with intuition
because balanced thinking has huge benefits, like improved clarity. Your
mind and intuition working together opens you to new ideas and
opportunities. Many times when my mind is stuck on some question, if I
give up thinking about it, the answer will suddenly appear. When your
mind is balanced it’s easier to sense energy. If you stop thinking what
you should see, you’ll be amazed at what you do see. For example, I had
this student in LA and I was teaching about how to see the world. And
she’s, you know, working with this other student. And she says, “I can’t
see any energy in the aura.” So I went around behind her, and I just
looked over her shoulder, and I looked at her reading screen. This is
kind of a little teacher’s trick, right? So I could see what she was
seeing intuitively. And I said, “Well, what about all those flowers,
that beautiful floral print around the person?” And she said, “Oh, well,
you didn’t tell us to see that. Is that the aura? I see that all the
time.” So balanced thinking really helps get through these preconceived
notions. And balanced thinking can also improve our relationships. We
become a better listener with deeper understanding. For example, you
might be listening to your partner about some detailed frustrations, or
worries, or complaints. And then suddenly because you’re using your
intuition, boom, you get the bigger picture. My partner needs to hear
three things. I love you. I’m not going to leave you and it’s not your
fault. And even though they’re not talking about those things at all,
you try it out and you say them, and it works, and they feel better.
This is a real example from my life. Balanced thinking also creates less
stress in your body. As my mind calmed down, I began recovering from my
adrenal fatigue. So how do you do it? How do you turn down the analyzer?
So we can make this really simple because energy follows your intention.
Try this out while I’m talking, either with your eyes open or closed.
Without any effort, notice how active your mind is right now. And now
imagine there’s a little light switch or a volume knob on your analyzer.
You can just see it or feel it. It doesn’t matter. Just turn it down to
about 50%. And notice what’s happening. Okay, try turning it down to
30%. Turn your analyzer down to 10%. Try turning it off. This is a very
simple way to turn your analyzer down. You don’t need to see the switch
or the knob visually, I don’t. Just know that you can turn things down.
Bzz. Zzz. Zzz. Zzs. It’s that easy. So I remember a funny story from a
friend of Mindvalley who tried this. She was studying the Tibetan

and then define the English equivalent in one of these three big

adjusting that analyzer to get something done. There was just too much
information for her mind to process, but her intuition could do it

your mind is right now. Just give it a number from zero to 100%. And now
imagine a light switch or a volume knob for your analyzer. And adjust it
to about 50% and notice what happens. Now try 80%. Back to 50%, Try 30%.
10%. Just try turning your analyzer off. Just let it be fast and easy.
Now let it adjust automatically to your most comfortable setting. Any
setting is okay. And keep in mind that on and off are both good settings
for the analyzer, just like lights in your house. Sometimes you want
them on. Sometimes you want them off. With the analyzer, we’re looking
for balance. So when they’re on, we get details and precision, you see
the trees. When it’s off, we’re seeing the big picture. We see the
forest. When it’s on, we’re assembling information. When it’s off, we
get a holistic understanding. This is why thinking alone can result in
poor decisions because we’re not seeing the big picture. When the
analyzer’s on, we can plan how to get somewhere. But when it’s off, we
know where to go. When it’s on, it’s great for writing software, but

secret.” So both settings are great. You can learn when to use each one
and then use them in balance. So now you can see why the analyzer is
great for physical perception, but not so good for energy perception. So
physical perception feels real. It’s specific, and detailed, and static,
and like text and a book, you know, it’s the same each time. And
physical perception helps you assemble parts into a greater
understanding and you have tons of practice at it. That’s why it feels
so real. Energy perception on the other hand is more like a dream, like
in a dream, you’re driving a car, and then you’re riding a bike, and

patterns. Like my friend’s a good example. He’s a hang glider. And he
has lots of experience looking at the clouds. So where I don’t see

moisture, all these different things because he’s practiced a lot. And
you’ll begin noticing energy patterns too as you practice. So energy

she’d been seeing auras her whole life as beautiful flowers and patterns
around people. But when I asked her to see an aura, she said, “I can’t
do it.” It’s not what she expected. Your energy perception is probably
the same way. You’re already doing it, but you don’t know it. Your mind
has convinced you otherwise. So today is all about overthinking. So I’ve

LESSON 8: Learn How to Clear Your Mental Distractions

<v ->Welcome back. Give yourself a deep breath. And as we begin, please
remember your grounding. Turn down your analyzer, and say hello to the

for you to make it more fun. Now, I love drawing energy cartoons because
they help you keep your analyzer turned down. Let’s take a look. How can
I read energy? First, I’ll say that sometimes it does help to think of
energy like an object. So imagine all the information in the universe is
available in a big book in the sky. We’re going to call this book the
Akashic records, where all information is available, where everything is
connected. This is an inaccurate analogy, but it helps. In truth, these
answers are available, not in one place, but in every place. With
energy, all information is available all the time, everywhere. That’s
why I love questions and answers. If someone in class asks me a question
about energy, I just look up the answer and respond. I was doing Q&A one
time for my intuition training, and a long-time student asked, “How do

you forget which class you’re in? I don’t know these answers. But when
people ask me questions, it’s like someone hands me a card with a
question on one side and the answer on the other. I just flip it over
and read it. It’s easy. That’s intuition.” So what gets in the way of
tuning into this infinite information and intelligence? We talked about
the big one already: thoughts and overthinking. You can’t stop thinking
about the past or you’re worried about the future, or there’s a critic
or judge that’s narrating your life. This is too big or too small or too
stupid or too smart. This is very distracting. What else gets in the way
of tuning into your intuition? Other people’s words and ideas, social
norms. Am I liked and accepted? What should I be saying and thinking? It
can be fun to fit in, to say and think the same things, but that doesn’t
mean they’re true. When we start using intuition, we often ask
ourselves, does what I see energetically match the group norm? And if
not, we doubt ourselves. We sense that we’re being judged by other
people and this makes it hard to sense energy. So, what else gets in the
way of tuning into your intuition? Your memories. They can seem so clear
and so real. Let’s say you remember a conversation with your friend from
years ago. And you remember that she was pregnant and you remember you
said something brilliant. And you remember that you were petting her
cat. But then if you think a little bit more about it, you realize, oh,
wait a sec, that friend didn’t live in the same place as that cat. And
actually, maybe my friend said the brilliant thing and not me. And then
this is the problem. When we remember things we do just that: we
re-member them. We reassemble pieces of information, and then we pretend
that they all happened together. But sometimes they don’t. Have you
noticed that? I first noticed when I was in college. I lived in Socorro,
New Mexico, and I was bragging to my girlfriend, trying to look smart.
And I told her “socorro” means health in Spanish. And I know, because I

“Socorro, socorro.” And my girlfriend nodded her head. She said, “Yeah,
that’s fascinating. But I actually speak Spanish and socorro means help,
not health.” And on the spot, my memory changed. This cartoon nurse
turned into a little girl who was calling for help. “Socorro, socorro.”
And I was shocked. It’s like, my brain is unreliable. So sometimes it’s
good to doubt yourself a little bit. Your memories are unreliable, too.
And police say this about eyewitnesses, that they’re notorious for
conflicting stories. It was a blue car, it was a gray bus. There were
three people, there were four people, etc. And it’s because we’re
remembering or reassembling partial information. And of course, we
forget things, too. Many times, our memories are missing important
pieces. There’s little holes in our stories. And that’s why it can be
misleading to base our perception on our memories. So, that’s a lot of

a light switch and turn on the lights. What does your room look like or
feel like to you? Have you been here recently or is it old and
abandoned? Give yourself permission to see all the conscious and
unconscious information here. Let yourself see all your old thoughts and
ideas, everything you’re keeping in case you need it again. You might

is right for you. And as you become aware of these old thoughts, decide
if you really need to keep them, are they helping you or are they just
clutter? Create a huge grounding cord in the center of your head, in the

LESSON 10: How to Access Universal Wisdom

<v ->Welcome back. Give yourself a deep breath. And as we begin, please
remember your grounding and be in the center of your head. Might feel a

Akashic records is a term used to describe how the universe is
organized, so all information is available from anywhere. Not in a book
or somewhere else, it’s actually inside us because it’s inside
everything. We are each connected to the whole on a quantum level, it’s

LESSON 13: Why Do We Struggle & Get Sick?

<v ->Welcome everyone, it’s Jeffrey Allen again. As we begin please
remember your grounding. Turn down your analyzer. And be in the center
of your head. Say hello to the group energy. Send smiles and hellos to
your fellow students. And feel the group energy and intention supporting
you. Good. In this chapter we’re learning about healing your body, which
is a huge topic. Of course with the body our first thought is usually to
take a physical approach. What’s the magic pill or supplement or diet or
exercise? Now, I’m not a doctor and I can’t help you with that approach,
but here’s what I can do, I can help you understand why you get sick
energetically and how to change that pattern. In my experience, healing
will occur naturally if you make room. So we’ll be learning about
managing your energy in a healthy way, energy tools for staying healthy,
energy tools for healing yourself and others, and using energy work with
traditional medicine. Now this last one is really important, when people
learn energy healing and start getting results, they often think, wow,
this is great, I’ll never need medicine again, or I’ll never need to go
to the doctor again. And I’m telling you now this is not true. Energy
work is not a replacement for physical treatment or medicine, but they
do work great together. Now, I’m not saying this because a lawyer told
me to, I’m saying it because I made this mistake when I learned about
energy healing. I stopped going to doctors, I canceled all my insurance
and years later I regretted it. My life would have been easier had I
used both like I do now, and I don’t want you to make the same mistake,
but I am really excited to teach you about energy healing and help you
find that balance. So the first rule of energy healing is that healing
is natural. Life is naturally healing and organizing and moving toward
coherency. Your body knows how to heal itself. If you clear the energy
miracles can happen. This can be on a small scale, like back pain or a
headache. Oftentimes if you clear the energy you’ll get instant relief.
Or this can be on a larger scale with some acute physical symptoms. I’ll
tell you kind of a fun story. My daughter when she was little, my
daughter, Mariah, she was walking between me and her mom and she walked
right into a pole and it had a little screw on it it just went right
into her forehead, and so right away she had a bump starting to form and
a little cut there that was red, and her mom and I both did energy
healing. So we just sat her down, got on my knee, and just said, you
know, started doing a little bit of energy healing and I didn’t really
know what to do, but I just asked myself what needs to happen here. And
so just intuitively I started kind of moving my hand, pulling out the
energy that said there was an injury, imagining I was kind of stitching
it up with some little energy thread and so on. And within a couple
minutes, the bump went away, the red was gone and there was just like a
tiny line there, where you could see that she’d been hit. So it was
amazing, and this is when I realized how easy healing can be. Anyone can
do this, just imagine that you know how. And in the moment when you need
it, you’ll find that clarity of just, what can I do to help? And the
answer will just come to you, it’s really easy. So if healing is natural
like this, what goes wrong? What’s the number one reason that we
struggle with healing and personal growth? Why don’t we keep up with our
fitness programs and our diets and healing sessions and personal growth
programs? The reason is we don’t know how to handle the growth that
comes from rapid healing. This is why we stagnate our growth. This is
why we drop out of the programs which can help us the most. So how many
of you have taken a new exercise program or a new diet and then felt
fantastic at first and swore that you’ll continue it for life. And you
were so excited and so committed and then two to three months in you
hate it and you drop out, how many times have you done that? I know I
have. So why did this happen? Well, your biggest growth period comes
when your biggest acceleration is occurring. We are great when we’re
feeling up, but we don’t know how to recover when we’re feeling down.
And understanding this can help you not burn out or drop out or blow up.
Energetically we call the situation a growth period. And let me give you
an example of a bad growth period or maybe I should say a normal growth
period, ’cause they’re usually pretty bad if we don’t handle them
energetically. So I was really interested in trying out yoga when I
lived in Denver, and I went for something extreme, some kind of an
extremist, so I went to Bikram Yoga, which is this super hot, sweaty
kind of power yoga, and I was gone just a little bit, you know, kind of
here and there, they were actually teasing me that I had the oldest
punch card anybody had ever see ’cause I had showed up so infrequently.
And then they put out a challenge and I love challenges. They said, if
you go six times a week for 10 weeks, it’ll change your life. And so I
signed right up, I got into it, and for the first few weeks I loved it,
it was fantastic. And then pretty quickly I started to hate it, I was
super angry about the heat, just wanted to kill somebody for not turning

know, I stuck with it and I finished the 10 weeks and I got great
results, but I never went again, like I never, ever wanted to do yoga
again, which is too bad ’cause it was really healthy. And a bad growth
period looks like this. First, you ask for personal growth when you’re
feeling good, and then the easy energy starts to release and you’re
feeling great. And then the stuck energy starts to release, and you get
grumpy and you get overwhelmed. And this is where we often make a big
mistake. We engage our analyzer to solve this. So we feel disappointed
or defensive, so we try to identify the culprit. Was it this person or
something on TV or my job or the doctor, that exercise instructor, then
we quit or attack the culprit, and we feel really self-righteous about
it. So we blame our partner or boss or teacher, etc. And unfortunately
this actually feels pretty good because we’re releasing some energy, so

growth period, does this sound familiar? So I’ve done this so many times
and I’m sure you have to, and this can happen with personal growth
programs too. So let’s look a little deeper at what are the results of a
growth period like this? So in general your life gets more difficult
with big ups and downs. You reinforce your pain instead of releasing it,

blaming. This will reduce your negative energy and your negative

LESSON 17 - BONUS VIDEO: Energy healing fast start guide

- The good news is that everybody is a healer on an energy level. The first thing, is what I mentioned already, is you want to identify what the problem is. So this is the thing I'm working on. If it's physical, it's a little bit obvious. You know, I'm working on this cut or some pain in the body. If it's emotional or just a pattern you're trying to change in your life, you can still identify it. You can say, "I've got this pattern around money and that's the one I really want to change." So you know, you identify that. Second step is you give yourself permission to see what's really going on because these patterns are unconscious, and oftentimes, they're unconscious because there was some pain that happened and so now you've surrounded that whole event with a little unconscious energy to stop your attention from going there and getting in pain again. So healing is not always this kind of feel good journey, right? If you've got a deep pattern that's difficult for you, there's probably some difficulty in there. So you got to give yourself permission to experience that. It's okay. I'm going to go in, and I'm going to look deeper. And oftentimes, what you'll find is that when you go, look, you've grown up since you had that injury. Things that are traumatic when you're 10 years old don't seem as traumatic when you're a little bit older, from an adult perspective. You look back, "Yeah, I can see how that was traumatic, but I can kind of also see some of the other circumstances, and it's not as big a deal as it was back then." You'll find the same thing. So give yourself permission to really look at that honestly for yourself and find out what's happening inside. So the third part there is you're going to want to expand your awareness of this topic. So let's use this money example. So I've decided I'm going to focus on money. Why isn't my money going to where I want it to go? And then I'm giving myself permission to really see what's happening there. And then I'm going to let my awareness just kind of expand to what's the backstory, what could be happening? Just let that information come in. I might start to notice, "Oh, my uncle had a lot of money and my uncle was kind of a jerk. So I made an association somewhere that having money meant that I was going to be like my uncle, and I don't want to be like him 'cause he is kind of a jerk." I'm not talking about my uncle. An unnecessary coupling of that energy and I'm ready to change it. Whatever comes to you. Remember, you've got this intelligence inside. You know how to do energy healing already. So now that you've done this healing work and got that information, you want to do a little expansion. So what I mean by that is you want to get the stuff that's nearby. So these energy patterns, they're not quite that cut and dry, right? So if you've got a pattern around money, it's not just because your uncle had money and he was a jerk. That might be the core thing or the thing you start with. Part 4: Empathy & Healthy Personal Boundaries

LESSON 19: Why Is Energy Contagious?

<v ->Welcome everyone. It’s Jeffrey Allen again. As we begin, please
remember you’re grounding. And be in the center of your head, and notice
your earth and cosmic energy running. Say hello to the group energy and
send smiles and hellos to your fellow students, and feel the group
energy and intention supporting you. Good. Today we’ll be exploring
empathy and healthy personal boundaries. Empathy is one of the most
interesting and most misunderstood areas of intuition. From an energy
perspective, we are constantly emerged in a sea of thoughts, ideas,
emotions, and feelings from other people. Yet, just like the fish in the
sea, we are often completely unaware of the water we swim in and how
much it affects us. Empathy is the energetic skill we use to match and
merge with this sea of energy that’s all around us. Our personal
boundaries determine if this is a healthy process, which we feel good
with, or if we feel overwhelmed by this out of control empathy. In
simple terms, boundaries mean you get to choose. In the physical world,
sometimes you have to do things that you don’t want. You have to follow
the rules, even the dumb ones, and people with size or power can push
you around. But this is not true in the energy world. In the energy
world, you get to choose which energies you experience. No one can
impose their energy on you if you understand boundaries and seniority.
The term seniority just means that you understand that this is true,
that you get to choose your energy. Think about how we transfer energy
in the physical and energy worlds, they’re very different. The physical
world deals with finite objects. If I give you an object, now you have
it and I no longer have it. If I talk you into carrying my suitcase and
guitar, now I don’t have to carry them, and maybe this is okay because
you wanted to help me. By contrast, the energy world deals with the
infinite. It’s more like transferring frequencies or transferring energy
and than transferring objects. If I give you some information, now you
have a copy, but I still have the original. Let’s say I talk you into
carrying my emotional baggage, now we’re both carrying it. You didn’t
really help me or yourself. Empathy is about learning to match or use
another energy, and energetically we really have infinite potential. We
can learn or become anything. A good analogy is to imagine that you are
the guitar, right? And you can play any song. If I teach you my song,
you can play it and so can I. So how does energy travel from person to
person? You can think of energy like waves or sounds rather than
particles or objects. You are a beautiful guitar with infinite potential
and you vibrate your song out in the world. Good and bad, fears and
pains, happiness. These songs are like tuning forks ringing at a precise
note. Other people also have infinite potential. They have matching
tuning forks. When you play your song, the energy travels to them and
they vibrate at your song. Your vibration is now part of them and vice
versa, at least temporarily. They have learned to play your song. It
doesn’t matter if it’s a good song or a bad song, that’s empathy,
matching the energy around you. It’s not simply thinking I can relate.
Empathy isn’t a mental understanding, it’s actually becoming the energy
temporarily, and we all do this, mostly unconsciously. Our energy
boundaries determine how often and how it affects us. The technical term
for this is sympathetic resonance. It happens when there is harmonic

LESSON 21: Who’s in Control of Your Life?

LESSON 26: What Are The Chakras?

<v ->Welcome back. Give yourself a deep breath. And, as we begin, please
remember your grounding. Relax into the center of your head, and notice
your Earth and Cosmic energy running. Say hello to your permission rose,
and say hello to the group energy. Send smiles and hellos to your fellow
students, and feel the group energy and intention supporting you. Ah,
very good. To understand your chakras, first, think about your physical
body. Your physical body is organized with organs for complex functions,
like the liver, the heart, the brain, each with a different function,
and with glands, or simple organs, that synthesize and store fluids.
Your energy body is organized, too. Chakras are like the organs of the
energy body. We have seven main chakras in the body, and each one
processes a different kind of energy. You’ve already worked with the
root and the crown chakra. We also have minor chakras in our hands and
our feet and our knees that help adjust our energy flow. So what are
these chakras anyway, and why do we have them? To me, chakras are like
your personal orchestra. They’re listening attentively and sensitive to
the energy all around you. And they’re changing and adapting, adjusting
based on your programs. And they’re broadcasting energy, sending your
song back to the world. In this analogy, chakras are like speakers and
the aura is like music coming from the speakers. Chakras worked best in
harmony, like the strings on a guitar. They can sound fantastic if
tuned. Just imagine that really yummy person. They probably have tuned
chakras. And they can sound kind of horrible if they’re not tuned. Have
you ever thought, “Something’s off with that person”? It’s likely they
have a little stuck energy in a chakra. It’s probably not just a
personality problem. Just like having a string out of tune, if you’re
chakras are off, it just sounds wrong. But, like a guitar, it’s fixable.
Your chakras are always sending your song into the world, so you want
them to sound good, right? When we look at the seven main chakras, each
has a different function. As I describe them, just put your hands in
front of your chakra. Let yourself feel it as I talk and get an
experiential understanding. Okay, so the seven chakras are numbered from
bottom to top. The root chakra is down by the base of the spine, and it
has to do with physical survival, health and money. You really want to
have a solid foundation here, which is why we started with grounding,
working on that root chakra. Your second chakra is right here, kind of
in the navel, and it deals with emotions, sexuality, and vitality. And
as you tune into this chakra right now, just ask yourself, “Do I have a
powerful fire burning in me? Do I have that motivation and passion that
moves things forward?” That’s second chakra energy. The third chakra is
in the solar plexus, and this has to do with manifesting, personal
power, taking action, and control. As you feel it right now, notice what
your third chakra feels like. Does it feel like you can accomplish your
goals? Do you have the power needed to take action in the world? Your
fourth chakra is your heart chakra, and it has to do with love for
yourself and others. And as you feel it, just ask yourself, “Am I fully
able to give love? Am I fully able to receive love?” That’s the dominant
energy in the fourth chakra. Okay, moving up toward the throat, you’ll
find the fifth chakra, which governs communication. And as you feel it,
ask yourself, “Can I speak my truth? Do I feel free to say what I want
and not be afraid what others think?” That’s what a strong fifth chakra
feels like. The sixth chakra in the forehead is about intuition and
guidance. And, often, it’s called the third eye. So just feel it for
yourself right now and ask, “Do I feel confident that I can see energy
and understand energy and receive my guidance?” That’s all coming from
the sixth chakra. Your seventh chakra is your crown chakra. We work with
this for the Cosmic energy, and it has to do with inspiration and your
spiritual connection. So do I feel connected spiritually? The crown
chakra is also the gateway to the upper dimensions. You actually have 12
energy centers, but five of them are out of the body. And we don’t talk
about those very much, because we’re still trying to get a grasp of
these seven that are in the body, but you can explore those upper
chakras on your own if you like. Just feeling them. The seventh chakra
is also a little different because it faces upward, like a crown or a
halo, but you can also feel it front to back, just like the other
chakras. So, hopefully, you could feel the differences between your
chakras already, because they have different energies. Some might feel a
little stronger or a little weaker or be a little more clear or more
vague. And maybe you felt some that were a little out of tune. At this
point, just be curious about your chakras and we’ll learn to adjust them
later. While I personally think feeling your chakras is the best way to
master them, I want to share a little more detailed too, just to satisfy

LESSON 29: Break Your Manifestation Blocks

<v ->Welcome back, give yourself a deep breath. And as we begin, please
remember your grounding and Earth energy, and relax into the center of

our ideas into physical form. So what’s happening energetically when we
manifest easily and what’s happening when we don’t. Now, you may
remember in the common manifesting pattern that I mentioned earlier,
where you get a fantastic idea and you can’t stop thinking about it. And
you talk to your friends and you have lots of enthusiasm and passion and
planning, and then you buy a domain name and then nothing. So what went
wrong? Let’s look at the energy. Now, energy actually manifests from the
seventh chakra down all the way through to the first, going through
chakra by chakra. So it’s pure energy or spirit manifesting into solid
form into the physical world. Each chakra plays an important role and
you need all your chakras working to manifest well. If your energy gets
stuck or stops in a particular chakra, your manifestation will stop
there too. This is why your projects always get stuck in the same place.
They’re stuck in the same chakra. So all your chakras are needed for big
success. So the real question is which chakra are you getting stuck in?
If you understand this, you can address that chakra’s block. So take a
guess. Which chakra would you think you’re stuck in? You might be
surprised. I know I was. Like I said, everything you create manifests in
seven distinct phases, so one per chakra. And each stage is important
and it has to happen for you to successfully manifest something in the
world. So let’s go through the stages. So first is the crown chakra at
the top of the head. So you receive inspiration and ideas, and this is
pure energy and spirit and opportunity coming in. Then it travels down
to your sixth chakra, which is in the head. This is when you’re filling
in all the details and dreaming and thinking and getting guidance and so
on. And then the energy comes down into the throat, the fifth chakra.
And this is where you’re communicating, where you’re writing or telling
people or talking about it. And the energy comes down into the heart, to
the fourth chakra. And this is where you’re getting all this enthusiasm
and passion and motivation. And you’re just loving it so much that you
have to do it. And the energy keeps going down into your solar plexus,
into the third chakra. And this is really where you’re planting the seed
and you’re taking action. So you’re making it possible for this idea or
inspiration to manifest in the physical world. Then the energy comes
down into the navel, into the second chakra. And this is where you get
your fuel for building and energizing and nurturing, like all the steps
that are needed to burn this idea into physical reality and to nurture
it to life. Finally, the energy moves down into your root chakra, near
the base of your spine. And this is really for rooting and sustaining.
So once your project is rooted, it has a life of its own and it’s
sustainable even without you. And this is when you’re completely done.
You’re actually free at this point to walk away and to do something new,

linear. It’s common to be working on more than one stage concurrently,
but if you get stuck somewhere, your project will stall and you can get
stuck in each of these phases. If you gets stuck up here in the crown,
you’re not going to feel inspired. You have no clue what to do. Maybe
you’ve got writer’s block. If you gets stuck in the sixth chakra, you
can’t imagine how to do it. Or maybe you think it’s impossible. If you
get stuck in the fifth chakra, in the throat, you might be afraid to
talk about your ideas, maybe someone will judge you or you’ll get in
trouble. And so it stays a secret desire. If the energy gets stuck in
your heart chakra, you just can’t motivate yourself. You can’t really
decide you’re going to go for it. So you keep playing small. If energy

That’s actually planning. I know because I own many unused domain names.

right? And instead, ask, what belief am I holding onto? And is this
belief useful? If it is, great, keep it, but if it’s not, let it go.
This will change your world. Enjoy.

LESSON 39: What Is Intuition?

<v ->Welcome back, give yourself a deep breath. And as we begin, please
remember your grounding and Earth energy. Relax into the center of your
head. Your analyzer off. Say hello to your Permission Rose and create a
new one if needed. And notice your Cosmic energy running energizing your
chakras. Say hello to the group energy. Send smiles and hellos to your
fellow students and feel the group energy and intention supporting you.
So let’s talk a little more about intuition myths. We already talked
about myth number one, which is that intuition is found only in some
special people and you’re not one of them. This is not true, everyone
can and is using their intuition. Myth number two, is that intuition is
an additional dormant sixth sense, kind of like intuition as a special
case. And the opposite is actually true. Physical perception is a
special case. Let me see if I can make this simple. So we all agree that
everything is energy, right? E equals MC squared. And physical matter is
a special case of energy. So certain frequencies that are localized in
time and space. Localized just means focused or restricted to a specific
time and space. That’s all the word physical means, time and space
relative. It follows that physical perception is a special case of
energy perception. Think about your body senses, they’re all localized
in time and space just like physical matter. Sight, sound, smell, touch,
taste they’re all about here and now because your body is your lens into
the here and now. Intuition is a broader case of energy perception. It’s
not localized, it’s not restricted in time and space. It’s actually all
the same senses without this time space restriction. So you can see,
hear, feel, smell, taste energy in the past, the present, the future
here, there, everywhere. Intuition is not really your sixth sense, it’s
your five senses with the gloves taken off. So let’s look at an example
like colors are a specific frequency in the visible light spectrum like
yellow is around 530 terahertz. Yet people consistently see colors in
the chakras and aura, but the aura isn’t in the visible light spectrum,

different people agree that they see yellow, but they aren’t actually
seeing yellow in the physical world? Well, light frequencies are the
physical expression of color per we see in the physical world, but color
is more than just the light frequencies and you can sense it. So is
hearing, taste, smell, and touch. This is why it’s difficult for people
to know if they’re using their intuition. It’s not radically different
from your physical senses. It just kind of seems real even though it’s
not physical. That’s why we say things like, I saw this in your aura or

energetically. But we didn’t use our eyes, our ears or our hands for

even home. Or you can swear that you got touched by somebody, but
nobody’s there. It feels so real because it is real. It’s just happening
beyond your body’s limited awareness. So what is intuition anyway? Now,

is just sensing energy without physical body limitations. This gives you
a broad time perspective. You can sense what’s happening right now, both

it’s a probability of space and it can change. The purpose of reading

LESSON 49: Duality Graduation & Continuing Your Journey

<v ->Welcome back. Give yourself a deep breath, and without effort, find
your space. Remember your grounding, center of your head, your Earth and
Cosmic energy running. Your aura boundary and your permission rose. Say
hello to your higher self and feel all the guides around you, loving you
and supporting you. It can be this easy to tune in. Just remember your
energy tools and your higher awareness. Today is our final lesson for
Duality. Wow, what a journey it’s been. Thank you for all the time and
practice and love that you put in. And thank you for trusting me to take
you on this journey. It’s been an honor. There are so many ways to
continue accessing your higher guidance. You can connect with your
higher self by looking at a mirror, or in a meditation of your own
design. You might travel upward from your crown like we did before, or
imagine that you’re sitting on a throne, or anything else, which feels
connecting to you. Just trust yourself and explore and discover the best
ways for you. Just keep expanding, but don’t get lost. Remember, you’re
in this life for a reason. If you start thinking, I only want to be a
spirit or I want to go home or I want to escape this life, these are not
the thoughts of an integrated body and spirit identity. Remember to
ground, run your energy, and clear that growth period. Integrate your
physical and energy identity: your body and your spirit. It’s not one or
the other. Have them both, love them both. Have enough energy presence
to enjoy a higher perspective. That little smile that says, hmm, I know
there’s something bigger. And have enough physical presence to live this
life fully. Remember the end of the meditation? I love my higher self. I
love my human self. This is the essence of Duality awareness. There are
so many ways to connect and communicate with your spirit guides, too.
The two methods we tried, work well for many people, but feel free to
explore and invent your own. With time, it will become easy and natural
as you find and develop your strengths. My strength is my clear
audience. So I don’t try to see my guides, I just talk to them and they
respond. Your guidance might come as pure inspiration, like when I was
organizing Duality. When I’m connecting with my higher self and guides,
it feels easy and flowing, not thinking too much. Or you might connect
with them through guided writing. Just to say hello and begin to write
or type. Don’t think: just keep going until there’s nothing more to
write. I wrote for four full days once, a whole book’s worth of
material. And it was fascinating to read later because I didn’t remember
most of it. Or if clairvoyance is strong for you, you might see your
guides. I was sitting in my car in Boulder one day, and I looked over to
see my guide in the passenger seat. She was so beautiful. I just broke
out in tears; it was so amazing. It’s very rare for me. Journeys with
your guides can be very powerful too. In Sedona, I had a deep meditation
practice for communicating with animals and the angelic realm and the
elemental realm. And every morning, I’d see Pegasus, the winged horse,
and I’d get on his back and we’d journey together. Now, I have no idea
why I was seeing Pegasus, but we traveled everywhere: inside the body,
around the planet, other worlds and dimensions. And all the while with
this verbal commentary. And afterwards, I’d tell my roommate, “Wow, that
was the most amazing meditation ever.” And Ken would say, “Again?”
Because it happened every day. Higher guidance is pretty addicting, in a
good way. My longest stretch was over 500 mornings in a row. I totally
loved it. Now remember, your communication will be unique to you and
your guides. With practice, you’ll discover a style that works great for
you. And then I recommend sticking with it every day. You don’t need a
goal; just one day at a time. I never set out to reach 500 days. I was
just having fun and it went by. If your meditation is fascinating to
you, it’s really easy. Otherwise, it probably won’t last very long. And
even the most fascinating experiences eventually give way to other
passions and endeavors. So don’t be disappointed if that happens. There
are so many benefits of accessing your higher self and spirit guides.
You show up more powerfully in your life. You have a deeper
understanding of yourself in your life. More presence and depth of
character. Your relationships get deeper too. More compassion for those
around you. And you see beyond their pain and their masks. You’re more
sensitive to other people’s needs. You’ll also notice easier transitions
in life and not fighting with the flow. You’re getting advanced news
when you need it. And there’s less stress from unexpected or
misunderstood things. And you’ll have creative ideas with surprising
results. You’ll find solutions you couldn’t even imagine on your own.
Higher awareness also gives this amazing warm feeling of always being
loved and supported. I love this, especially in our times. We’re never
truly alone. You’ll also find a deep sense of joy and amusement, which
comes from peeking behind the scenes, knowing there’s something bigger
happening, and that you’re a part of it. Trusting that it’s all
unfolding beautifully. And one surprise benefit is that you stop feeling
guilty. When you see things from a higher perspective, there’s no need
for guilt. You’ve done the best that you can in each moment, and that
was the point: to shine and learn and grow. Not to be perfect. So, I
have a few final practice tips. I recommend connecting with your higher
self and spirit guides in the morning. And you can use my 10, 30, or
60-minute practice meditations to get started, and then just continue on
your own. And as you get guidance, even if you’re not sure, I recommend
trusting it and following it. The best way to know if it’s valid is to
follow it. Otherwise, you just won’t know. You can also play with higher
mind awareness during the day. Try to be in your higher mind, feeling
love and light coming from your higher self as you do your normal daily
activities. This is really fun. And try asking your guides questions
during your normal day too. Higher awareness isn’t just for meditation.
That’s just to get you started. The real goal is to be always connected
and being the brightest you. As always, be gentle with your expectations
and self-evaluation. Sometimes, it may feel like you’ve failed. Like
your guidance steered you into a difficult situation. Whenever that
happens, I always realize later why the situation was perfect for me.
Maybe a key experience that I was resisting and wouldn’t have found on
my own. All these tips really boil down to one thing: let your higher
guidance be fun and easy. You might be thinking, sure Jeffrey, it’s easy
for you. But remember, I started right where you are. I remember when I
wanted to talk to my guides so bad, but thought I couldn’t do it. And I
remember when it came kind of fleetingly and randomly. And I spent a lot
of time clearing pictures and practicing with my energy tools and
intuition. And I got better. I could hear, but I wasn’t always certain.

certainty. Don’t worry, you can learn much faster than me. It doesn’t

give up. See what your results are then. A few things to watch out for
